{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_fast_colored_text_box_n_s_a31ffa48f01e78f0f694e4c152ca5e12c}{Highlighting\+Range\+Type}} Fast\+Colored\+Text\+Box\+NS.\+Fast\+Colored\+Text\+Box.\+Highlighting\+Range\+Type\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [get]}, {\ttfamily [set]}}



This property specifies which part of the text will be highlighted as you type (by built-\/in highlighter). 

When a user enters text, a component refreshes highlighting (because the text was changed). This property specifies exactly which section of the text will be re-\/highlighted. This can be useful to highlight multi-\/line comments, for example.\Hypertarget{class_fast_colored_text_box_n_s_1_1_fast_colored_text_box_a2d5620248d7baf270666dca7b2dfd050}\label{class_fast_colored_text_box_n_s_1_1_fast_colored_text_box_a2d5620248d7baf270666dca7b2dfd050}
